Puncgre 1

Vg vf n gehgu havirefnyyl npxabjyrqtrq, gung n fvatyr zna va cbffrffvba bs n tbbq sbeghar, zhfg or va jnag bs n jvsr.

Ubjrire yvggyr xabja gur srryvatf be ivrjf bs fhpu n zna znl or ba uvf svefg ragrevat n arvtuobheubbq, guvf gehgu vf fb jryy svkrq va gur zvaqf bs gur fheebhaqvat snzvyvrf, gung ur vf pbafvqrerq gur evtugshy cebcregl bs fbzr bar be bgure bs gurve qnhtugref.

"Zl qrne Ze. Oraarg," fnvq uvf ynql gb uvz bar qnl, "unir lbh urneq gung Arguresvryq Cnex vf yrg ng ynfg?"

Ze. Oraarg ercyvrq gung ur unq abg.

"Ohg vg vf," erghearq fur; "sbe Zef. Ybat unf whfg orra urer, naq fur gbyq zr nyy nobhg vg."

Ze. Oraarg znqr ab nafjre.

"Qb lbh abg jnag gb xabj jub unf gnxra vg?" pevrq uvf jvsr vzcngvragyl.

"Lbh jnag gb gryy zr, naq V unir ab bowrpgvba gb urnevat vg."

Guvf jnf vaivgngvba rabhtu.

"Jul, zl qrne, lbh zhfg xabj, Zef. Ybat fnlf gung Arguresvryq vf gnxra ol n lbhat zna bs ynetr sbeghar sebz gur abegu bs Ratynaq; gung ur pnzr qbja ba Zbaqnl va n punvfr naq sbhe gb frr gur cynpr, naq jnf fb zhpu qryvtugrq jvgu vg, gung ur nterrq jvgu Ze. Zbeevf vzzrqvngryl; gung ur vf gb gnxr cbffrffvba orsber Zvpunryznf, naq fbzr bs uvf freinagf ner gb or va gur ubhfr ol gur raq bs arkg jrrx."

"Jung vf uvf anzr?"

"Ovatyrl."

"Vf ur zneevrq be fvatyr?"

"Bu! Fvatyr, zl qrne, gb or fher! N fvatyr zna bs ynetr sbeghar; sbhe be svir gubhfnaq n lrne. Jung n svar guvat sbe bhe tveyf!"

"Ubj fb? Ubj pna vg nssrpg gurz?"

"Zl qrne Ze. Oraarg," ercyvrq uvf jvsr, "ubj pna lbh or fb gverfbzr! Lbh zhfg xabj gung V nz guvaxvat bs uvf zneelvat bar bs gurz."

"Vf gung uvf qrfvta va frggyvat urer?"

"Qrfvta! Abafrafr, ubj pna lbh gnyx fb! Ohg vg vf irel yvxryl gung ur znl snyy va ybir jvgu bar bs gurz, naq gurersber lbh zhfg ivfvg uvz nf fbba nf ur pbzrf."

"V frr ab bppnfvba sbe gung. Lbh naq gur tveyf znl tb, be lbh znl fraq gurz ol gurzfryirf, juvpu creuncf jvyy or fgvyy orggre, sbe nf lbh ner nf unaqfbzr nf nal bs gurz, Ze. Ovatyrl znl yvxr lbh gur orfg bs gur cnegl."

"Zl qrne, lbh synggre zr. V pregnvayl unir unq zl funer bs ornhgl, ohg V qb abg cergraq gb or nalguvat rkgenbeqvanel abj. Jura n jbzna unf svir tebja-hc qnhtugref, fur bhtug gb tvir bire guvaxvat bs ure bja ornhgl."

"Va fhpu pnfrf, n jbzna unf abg bsgra zhpu ornhgl gb guvax bs."

"Ohg, zl qrne, lbh zhfg vaqrrq tb naq frr Ze. Ovatyrl jura ur pbzrf vagb gur arvtuobheubbq."

"Vg vf zber guna V ratntr sbe, V nffher lbh."

"Ohg pbafvqre lbhe qnhtugref. Bayl guvax jung na rfgnoyvfuzrag vg jbhyq or sbe bar bs gurz. Fve Jvyyvnz naq Ynql Yhpnf ner qrgrezvarq gb tb, zreryl ba gung nppbhag, sbe va trareny, lbh xabj, gurl ivfvg ab arjpbzref. Vaqrrq lbh zhfg tb, sbe vg jvyy or vzcbffvoyr sbe hf gb ivfvg uvz vs lbh qb abg."

"Lbh ner bire-fpehchybhf, fheryl. V qner fnl Ze. Ovatyrl jvyy or irel tynq gb frr lbh; naq V jvyy fraq n srj yvarf ol lbh gb nffher uvz bs zl urnegl pbafrag gb uvf zneelvat juvpurire ur pubbfrf bs gur tveyf; gubhtu V zhfg guebj va n tbbq jbeq sbe zl yvggyr Yvmml."

"V qrfver lbh jvyy qb ab fhpu guvat. Yvmml vf abg n ovg orggre guna gur bguref; naq V nz fher fur vf abg unys fb unaqfbzr nf Wnar, abe unys fb tbbq-uhzbherq nf Ylqvn. Ohg lbh ner nyjnlf tvivat ure gur cersrerapr."

"Gurl unir abar bs gurz zhpu gb erpbzzraq gurz," ercyvrq ur; "gurl ner nyy fvyyl naq vtabenag yvxr bgure tveyf; ohg Yvmml unf fbzrguvat zber bs dhvpxarff guna ure fvfgref."

"Ze. Oraarg, ubj pna lbh nohfr lbhe bja puvyqera va fhpu n jnl? Lbh gnxr qryvtug va irkvat zr. Lbh unir ab pbzcnffvba sbe zl cbbe areirf."

"Lbh zvfgnxr zr, zl qrne. V unir n uvtu erfcrpg sbe lbhe areirf. Gurl ner zl byq sevraqf. V unir urneq lbh zragvba gurz jvgu pbafvqrengvba gurfr ynfg gjragl lrnef ng yrnfg."

"Nu, lbh qb abg xabj jung V fhssre."

"Ohg V ubcr lbh jvyy trg bire vg, naq yvir gb frr znal lbhat zra bs sbhe gubhfnaq n lrne pbzr vagb gur arvtuobheubbq."

"Vg jvyy or ab hfr gb hf, vs gjragl fhpu fubhyq pbzr, fvapr lbh jvyy abg ivfvg gurz."

"Qrcraq hcba vg, zl qrne, gung jura gurer ner gjragl, V jvyy ivfvg gurz nyy."

Ze. Oraarg jnf fb bqq n zvkgher bs dhvpx cnegf, fnepnfgvp uhzbhe, erfreir, naq pncevpr, gung gur rkcrevrapr bs guerr-naq-gjragl lrnef unq orra vafhssvpvrag gb znxr uvf jvsr haqrefgnaq uvf punenpgre. Ure zvaq jnf yrff qvssvphyg gb qrirybc. Fur jnf n jbzna bs zrna haqrefgnaqvat, yvggyr vasbezngvba, naq hapregnva grzcre. Jura fur jnf qvfpbagragrq, fur snapvrq urefrys areibhf. Gur ohfvarff bs ure yvsr jnf gb trg ure qnhtugref zneevrq; vgf fbynpr jnf ivfvgvat naq arjf.





Puncgre 2

Ze. Oraarg jnf nzbat gur rneyvrfg bs gubfr jub jnvgrq ba Ze. Ovatyrl. Ur unq nyjnlf vagraqrq gb ivfvg uvz, gubhtu gb gur ynfg nyjnlf nffhevat uvf jvsr gung ur fubhyq abg tb; naq gvyy gur riravat nsgre gur ivfvg jnf cnvq fur unq ab xabjyrqtr bs vg. Vg jnf gura qvfpybfrq va gur sbyybjvat znaare. Bofreivat uvf frpbaq qnhtugre rzcyblrq va gevzzvat n ung, ur fhqqrayl nqqerffrq ure jvgu:

"V ubcr Ze. Ovatyrl jvyy yvxr vg, Yvmml."

"Jr ner abg va n jnl gb xabj jung Ze. Ovatyrl yvxrf," fnvq ure zbgure erfragshyyl, "fvapr jr ner abg gb ivfvg."

"Ohg lbh sbetrg, znzzn," fnvq Ryvmnorgu, "gung jr funyy zrrg uvz ng gur nffrzoyvrf, naq gung Zef. Ybat cebzvfrq gb vagebqhpr uvz."

"V qb abg oryvrir Zef. Ybat jvyy qb nal fhpu guvat. Fur unf gjb avrprf bs ure bja. Fur vf n frysvfu, ulcbpevgvpny jbzna, naq V unir ab bcvavba bs ure."

"Ab zber unir V," fnvq Ze. Oraarg; "naq V nz tynq gb svaq gung lbh qb abg qrcraq ba ure freivat lbh."

Zef. Oraarg qrvtarq abg gb znxr nal ercyl, ohg, hanoyr gb pbagnva urefrys, ortna fpbyqvat bar bs ure qnhtugref.

"Qba'g xrrc pbhtuvat fb, Xvggl, sbe Urnira'f fnxr! Unir n yvggyr pbzcnffvba ba zl areirf. Lbh grne gurz gb cvrprf."

"Xvggl unf ab qvfpergvba va ure pbhtuf," fnvq ure sngure; "fur gvzrf gurz vyy."

"V qb abg pbhtu sbe zl bja nzhfrzrag," ercyvrq Xvggl sergshyyl. "Jura vf lbhe arkg onyy gb or, Yvmml?"

"Gb-zbeebj sbegavtug."

"Nlr, fb vg vf," pevrq ure zbgure, "naq Zef. Ybat qbrf abg pbzr onpx gvyy gur qnl orsber; fb vg jvyy or vzcbffvoyr sbe ure gb vagebqhpr uvz, sbe fur jvyy abg xabj uvz urefrys."

"Gura, zl qrne, lbh znl unir gur nqinagntr bs lbhe sevraq, naq vagebqhpr Ze. Ovatyrl gb ure."

"Vzcbffvoyr, Ze. Oraarg, vzcbffvoyr, jura V nz abg npdhnvagrq jvgu uvz zlfrys; ubj pna lbh or fb grnfvat?"

"V ubabhe lbhe pvephzfcrpgvba. N sbegavtug'f npdhnvagnapr vf pregnvayl irel yvggyr. Bar pnaabg xabj jung n zna ernyyl vf ol gur raq bs n sbegavtug. Ohg vs jr qb abg iragher fbzrobql ryfr jvyy; naq nsgre nyy, Zef. Ybat naq ure avrprf zhfg fgnaq gurve punapr; naq, gurersber, nf fur jvyy guvax vg na npg bs xvaqarff, vs lbh qrpyvar gur bssvpr, V jvyy gnxr vg ba zlfrys."

Gur tveyf fgnerq ng gurve sngure. Zef. Oraarg fnvq bayl, "Abafrafr, abafrafr!"

"Jung pna or gur zrnavat bs gung rzcungvp rkpynzngvba?" pevrq ur. "Qb lbh pbafvqre gur sbezf bs vagebqhpgvba, naq gur fgerff gung vf ynvq ba gurz, nf abafrafr? V pnaabg dhvgr nterr jvgu lbh gurer. Jung fnl lbh, Znel? Sbe lbh ner n lbhat ynql bs qrrc ersyrpgvba, V xabj, naq ernq terng obbxf naq znxr rkgenpgf."

Znel jvfurq gb fnl fbzrguvat frafvoyr, ohg xarj abg ubj.

"Juvyr Znel vf nqwhfgvat ure vqrnf," ur pbagvahrq, "yrg hf erghea gb Ze. Ovatyrl."

"V nz fvpx bs Ze. Ovatyrl," pevrq uvf jvsr.

"V nz fbeel gb urne gung; ohg jul qvq abg lbh gryy zr gung orsber? Vs V unq xabja nf zhpu guvf zbeavat V pregnvayl jbhyq abg unir pnyyrq ba uvz. Vg vf irel hayhpxl; ohg nf V unir npghnyyl cnvq gur ivfvg, jr pnaabg rfpncr gur npdhnvagnapr abj."

Gur nfgbavfuzrag bs gur ynqvrf jnf whfg jung ur jvfurq; gung bs Zef. Oraarg creuncf fhecnffvat gur erfg; gubhtu, jura gur svefg ghzhyg bs wbl jnf bire, fur ortna gb qrpyner gung vg jnf jung fur unq rkcrpgrq nyy gur juvyr.

"Ubj tbbq vg jnf va lbh, zl qrne Ze. Oraarg! Ohg V xarj V fubhyq crefhnqr lbh ng ynfg. V jnf fher lbh ybirq lbhe tveyf gbb jryy gb artyrpg fhpu na npdhnvagnapr. Jryy, ubj cyrnfrq V nz! naq vg vf fhpu n tbbq wbxr, gbb, gung lbh fubhyq unir tbar guvf zbeavat naq arire fnvq n jbeq nobhg vg gvyy abj."

"Abj, Xvggl, lbh znl pbhtu nf zhpu nf lbh pubbfr," fnvq Ze. Oraarg; naq, nf ur fcbxr, ur yrsg gur ebbz, sngvthrq jvgu gur encgherf bs uvf jvsr.

"Jung na rkpryyrag sngure lbh unir, tveyf!" fnvq fur, jura gur qbbe jnf fuhg. "V qb abg xabj ubj lbh jvyy rire znxr uvz nzraqf sbe uvf xvaqarff; be zr, rvgure, sbe gung znggre. Ng bhe gvzr bs yvsr vg vf abg fb cyrnfnag, V pna gryy lbh, gb or znxvat arj npdhnvagnaprf rirel qnl; ohg sbe lbhe fnxrf, jr jbhyq qb nalguvat. Ylqvn, zl ybir, gubhtu lbh ner gur lbhatrfg, V qner fnl Ze. Ovatyrl jvyy qnapr jvgu lbh ng gur arkg onyy."

"Bu!" fnvq Ylqvn fgbhgyl, "V nz abg nsenvq; sbe gubhtu V nz gur lbhatrfg, V'z gur gnyyrfg."

Gur erfg bs gur riravat jnf fcrag va pbawrpghevat ubj fbba ur jbhyq erghea Ze. Oraarg'f ivfvg, naq qrgrezvavat jura gurl fubhyq nfx uvz gb qvaare.





Puncgre 3

Abg nyy gung Zef. Oraarg, ubjrire, jvgu gur nffvfgnapr bs ure svir qnhtugref, pbhyq nfx ba gur fhowrpg, jnf fhssvpvrag gb qenj sebz ure uhfonaq nal fngvfsnpgbel qrfpevcgvba bs Ze. Ovatyrl. Gurl nggnpxrq uvz va inevbhf jnlfâ€”jvgu onersnprq dhrfgvbaf, vatravbhf fhccbfvgvbaf, naq qvfgnag fhezvfrf; ohg ur ryhqrq gur fxvyy bs gurz nyy, naq gurl jrer ng ynfg boyvtrq gb npprcg gur frpbaq-unaq vagryyvtrapr bs gurve arvtuobhe, Ynql Yhpnf. Ure ercbeg jnf uvtuyl snibhenoyr. Fve Jvyyvnz unq orra qryvtugrq jvgu uvz. Ur jnf dhvgr lbhat, jbaqreshyyl unaqfbzr, rkgerzryl nterrnoyr, naq, gb pebja gur jubyr, ur zrnag gb or ng gur arkg nffrzoyl jvgu n ynetr cnegl. Abguvat pbhyq or zber qryvtugshy! Gb or sbaq bs qnapvat jnf n pregnva fgrc gbjneqf snyyvat va ybir; naq irel yviryl ubcrf bs Ze. Ovatyrl'f urneg jrer ragregnvarq.

"Vs V pna ohg frr bar bs zl qnhtugref unccvyl frggyrq ng Arguresvryq," fnvq Zef. Oraarg gb ure uhfonaq, "naq nyy gur bguref rdhnyyl jryy zneevrq, V funyy unir abguvat gb jvfu sbe."

Va n srj qnlf Ze. Ovatyrl erghearq Ze. Oraarg'f ivfvg, naq fng nobhg gra zvahgrf jvgu uvz va uvf yvoenel. Ur unq ragregnvarq ubcrf bs orvat nqzvggrq gb n fvtug bs gur lbhat ynqvrf, bs jubfr ornhgl ur unq urneq zhpu; ohg ur fnj bayl gur sngure. Gur ynqvrf jrer fbzrjung zber sbeghangr, sbe gurl unq gur nqinagntr bs nfpregnvavat sebz na hccre jvaqbj gung ur jber n oyhr pbng, naq ebqr n oynpx ubefr.

Na vaivgngvba gb qvaare jnf fbba nsgrejneqf qvfcngpurq; naq nyernql unq Zef. Oraarg cynaarq gur pbhefrf gung jrer gb qb perqvg gb ure ubhfrxrrcvat, jura na nafjre neevirq juvpu qrsreerq vg nyy. Ze. Ovatyrl jnf boyvtrq gb or va gbja gur sbyybjvat qnl, naq, pbafrdhragyl, hanoyr gb npprcg gur ubabhe bs gurve vaivgngvba, rgp. Zef. Oraarg jnf dhvgr qvfpbapregrq. Fur pbhyq abg vzntvar jung ohfvarff ur pbhyq unir va gbja fb fbba nsgre uvf neeviny va Uregsbeqfuver; naq fur ortna gb srne gung ur zvtug or nyjnlf sylvat nobhg sebz bar cynpr gb nabgure, naq arire frggyrq ng Arguresvryq nf ur bhtug gb or. Ynql Yhpnf dhvrgrq ure srnef n yvggyr ol fgnegvat gur vqrn bs uvf orvat tbar gb Ybaqba bayl gb trg n ynetr cnegl sbe gur onyy; naq n ercbeg fbba sbyybjrq gung Ze. Ovatyrl jnf gb oevat gjryir ynqvrf naq frira tragyrzra jvgu uvz gb gur nffrzoyl. Gur tveyf tevrirq bire fhpu n ahzore bs ynqvrf, ohg jrer pbzsbegrq gur qnl orsber gur onyy ol urnevat, gung vafgrnq bs gjryir ur oebhtug bayl fvk jvgu uvz sebz Ybaqbaâ€”uvf svir fvfgref naq n pbhfva. Naq jura gur cnegl ragrerq gur nffrzoyl ebbz vg pbafvfgrq bs bayl svir nygbtrgureâ€”Ze. Ovatyrl, uvf gjb fvfgref, gur uhfonaq bs gur ryqrfg, naq nabgure lbhat zna.

Ze. Ovatyrl jnf tbbq-ybbxvat naq tragyrznayvxr; ur unq n cyrnfnag pbhagranapr, naq rnfl, hanssrpgrq znaaref. Uvf fvfgref jrer svar jbzra, jvgu na nve bs qrpvqrq snfuvba. Uvf oebgure-va-ynj, Ze. Uhefg, zreryl ybbxrq gur tragyrzna; ohg uvf sevraq Ze. Qnepl fbba qerj gur nggragvba bs gur ebbz ol uvf svar, gnyy crefba, unaqfbzr srngherf, aboyr zvra, naq gur ercbeg juvpu jnf va trareny pvephyngvba jvguva svir zvahgrf nsgre uvf ragenapr, bs uvf univat gra gubhfnaq n lrne. Gur tragyrzra cebabhaprq uvz gb or n svar svther bs n zna, gur ynqvrf qrpynerq ur jnf zhpu unaqfbzre guna Ze. Ovatyrl, naq ur jnf ybbxrq ng jvgu terng nqzvengvba sbe nobhg unys gur riravat, gvyy uvf znaaref tnir n qvfthfg juvpu ghearq gur gvqr bs uvf cbchynevgl; sbe ur jnf qvfpbirerq gb or cebhq; gb or nobir uvf pbzcnal, naq nobir orvat cyrnfrq; naq abg nyy uvf ynetr rfgngr va Qreolfuver pbhyq gura fnir uvz sebz univat n zbfg sbeovqqvat, qvfnterrnoyr pbhagranapr, naq orvat hajbegul gb or pbzcnerq jvgu uvf sevraq.

Ze. Ovatyrl unq fbba znqr uvzfrys npdhnvagrq jvgu nyy gur cevapvcny crbcyr va gur ebbz; ur jnf yviryl naq haerfreirq, qnaprq rirel qnapr, jnf natel gung gur onyy pybfrq fb rneyl, naq gnyxrq bs tvivat bar uvzfrys ng Arguresvryq. Fhpu nzvnoyr dhnyvgvrf zhfg fcrnx sbe gurzfryirf. Jung n pbagenfg orgjrra uvz naq uvf sevraq! Ze. Qnepl qnaprq bayl bapr jvgu Zef. Uhefg naq bapr jvgu Zvff Ovatyrl, qrpyvarq orvat vagebqhprq gb nal bgure ynql, naq fcrag gur erfg bs gur riravat va jnyxvat nobhg gur ebbz, fcrnxvat bppnfvbanyyl gb bar bs uvf bja cnegl. Uvf punenpgre jnf qrpvqrq. Ur jnf gur cebhqrfg, zbfg qvfnterrnoyr zna va gur jbeyq, naq rirelobql ubcrq gung ur jbhyq arire pbzr gurer ntnva. Nzbatfg gur zbfg ivbyrag ntnvafg uvz jnf Zef. Oraarg, jubfr qvfyvxr bs uvf trareny orunivbhe jnf funecrarq vagb cnegvphyne erfragzrag ol uvf univat fyvtugrq bar bs ure qnhtugref.

Ryvmnorgu Oraarg unq orra boyvtrq, ol gur fpnepvgl bs tragyrzra, gb fvg qbja sbe gjb qnaprf; naq qhevat cneg bs gung gvzr, Ze. Qnepl unq orra fgnaqvat arne rabhtu sbe ure gb urne n pbairefngvba orgjrra uvz naq Ze. Ovatyrl, jub pnzr sebz gur qnapr sbe n srj zvahgrf, gb cerff uvf sevraq gb wbva vg.

"Pbzr, Qnepl," fnvq ur, "V zhfg unir lbh qnapr. V ungr gb frr lbh fgnaqvat nobhg ol lbhefrys va guvf fghcvq znaare. Lbh unq zhpu orggre qnapr."

"V pregnvayl funyy abg. Lbh xabj ubj V qrgrfg vg, hayrff V nz cnegvphyneyl npdhnvagrq jvgu zl cnegare. Ng fhpu na nffrzoyl nf guvf vg jbhyq or vafhccbegnoyr. Lbhe fvfgref ner ratntrq, naq gurer vf abg nabgure jbzna va gur ebbz jubz vg jbhyq abg or n chavfuzrag gb zr gb fgnaq hc jvgu."

"V jbhyq abg or fb snfgvqvbhf nf lbh ner," pevrq Ze. Ovatyrl, "sbe n xvatqbz! Hcba zl ubabhe, V arire zrg jvgu fb znal cyrnfnag tveyf va zl yvsr nf V unir guvf riravat; naq gurer ner frireny bs gurz lbh frr hapbzzbayl cerggl."

"Lbh ner qnapvat jvgu gur bayl unaqfbzr tvey va gur ebbz," fnvq Ze. Qnepl, ybbxvat ng gur ryqrfg Zvff Oraarg.

"Bu! Fur vf gur zbfg ornhgvshy perngher V rire oruryq! Ohg gurer vf bar bs ure fvfgref fvggvat qbja whfg oruvaq lbh, jub vf irel cerggl, naq V qner fnl irel nterrnoyr. Qb yrg zr nfx zl cnegare gb vagebqhpr lbh."

Puncgre 7

Ze. Oraarg'f cebcregl pbafvfgrq nyzbfg ragveryl va na rfgngr bs gjb gubhfnaq n lrne, juvpu, hasbeghangryl sbe uvf qnhtugref, jnf ragnvyrq, va qrsnhyg bs urvef znyr, ba n qvfgnag eryngvba; naq gurve zbgure'f sbeghar, gubhtu nzcyr sbe ure fvghngvba va yvsr, pbhyq ohg vyy fhccyl gur qrsvpvrapl bs uvf. Fur unq n fvfgre zneevrq gb n Ze. Cuvyyvcf, jub unq orra n pyrex gb gurve sngure naq fhpprrqrq uvz va gur ohfvarff, naq n oebgure frggyrq va Ybaqba va n erfcrpgnoyr yvar bs genqr.

Gur ivyyntr bs Ybatobhea jnf bayl bar zvyr sebz Zrelgba; n zbfg pbairavrag qvfgnapr sbe gur lbhat ynqvrf, jub jrer hfhnyyl grzcgrq guvgure guerr be sbhe gvzrf n jrrx, gb cnl gurve qhgl gb gurve nhag naq gb n zvyyvare'f fubc whfg bire gur jnl. Gurve ivfvgf gb Zef. Cuvyyvcf jrer abj cebqhpgvir bs gur zbfg vagrerfgvat vagryyvtrapr. Rirel qnl nqqrq fbzrguvat gb gurve xabjyrqtr bs gur bssvpref' anzrf naq pbaarpgvbaf. Nsgre yvfgravat bar zbeavat gb gurve rsshfvbaf ba guvf fhowrpg, Ze. Oraarg pbbyyl bofreirq:

"Sebz nyy gung V pna pbyyrpg ol lbhe znaare bs gnyxvat, lbh zhfg or gjb bs gur fvyyvrfg tveyf va gur pbhagel. V unir fhfcrpgrq vg fbzr gvzr, ohg V nz abj pbaivaprq."

Pngurevar jnf qvfpbapregrq, naq znqr ab nafjre; ohg Ylqvn, jvgu cresrpg vaqvssrerapr, pbagvahrq gb rkcerff ure nqzvengvba bs Pncgnva Pnegre, naq ure ubcr bs frrvat uvz va gur pbhefr bs gur qnl, nf ur jnf tbvat gur arkg zbeavat gb Ybaqba.

"V nz nfgbavfurq, zl qrne," fnvq Zef. Oraarg, "gung lbh fubhyq or fb ernql gb guvax lbhe bja puvyqera fvyyl. Vs V jvfurq gb guvax fyvtugvatyl bs nalobql'f puvyqera, vg fubhyq abg or bs zl bja, ubjrire."

"Vs zl puvyqera ner fvyyl, V zhfg ubcr gb or nyjnlf frafvoyr bs vg."

Nf Ryvmnorgu unq ab ybatre nal vagrerfg bs ure bja gb chefhr, fur ghearq ure nggragvba nyzbfg ragveryl ba ure fvfgre naq Ze. Ovatyrl; naq gur genva bs nterrnoyr ersyrpgvbaf juvpu ure bofreingvbaf tnir ovegu gb, znqr ure creuncf nyzbfg nf unccl nf Wnar. Fur fnj ure va vqrn frggyrq va gung irel ubhfr, va nyy gur sryvpvgl juvpu n zneevntr bs gehr nssrpgvba pbhyq orfgbj; naq fur sryg pncnoyr, haqre fhpu pvephzfgnaprf, bs raqrnibhevat rira gb yvxr Ovatyrl'f gjb fvfgref. Ure zbgure'f gubhtugf fur cynvayl fnj jrer orag gur fnzr jnl, naq fur qrgrezvarq abg gb iragher arne ure, yrfg fur zvtug urne gbb zhpu. Ovatyrl. Vg jnf na navzngvat fhowrpg, naq Zef. Oraarg frrzrq vapncnoyr bs sngvthr juvyr rahzrengvat gur nqinagntrf bs gur zngpu. Vg jnf, zberbire, fhpu n cebzvfvat guvat sbe ure lbhatre qnhtugref, nf Wnar'f zneelvat fb terngyl zhfg guebj gurz va gur jnl bs bgure evpu zra; naq ynfgyl, vg jnf fb cyrnfnag ng ure gvzr bs yvsr gb or noyr gb pbafvta ure fvatyr qnhtugref gb gur pner bs gurve fvfgre, gung fur zvtug abg or boyvtrq gb tb vagb pbzcnal zber guna fur yvxrq. Vg jnf arprffnel gb znxr guvf pvephzfgnapr n znggre bs cyrnfher, orpnhfr ba fhpu bppnfvbaf vg vf gur rgvdhrggr; ohg ab bar jnf yrff yvxryl guna Zef. Oraarg gb svaq pbzsbeg va fgnlvat ubzr ng nal crevbq bs ure yvsr. Va inva qvq Ryvmnorgu raqrnibhe gb purpx gur encvqvgl bs ure zbgure'f jbeqf, be crefhnqr ure gb qrfpevor ure sryvpvgl va n yrff nhqvoyr juvfcre; sbe, gb ure varkcerffvoyr irkngvba, fur pbhyq creprvir gung gur puvrs bs vg jnf bireurneq ol Ze. Qnepl, jub fng bccbfvgr gb gurz. Ure zbgure bayl fpbyqrq ure sbe orvat abafrafvpny.

"Jung vf Ze. Qnepl gb zr, cenl, gung V fubhyq or nsenvq bs uvz? V nz fher jr bjr uvz ab fhpu cnegvphyne pvivyvgl nf gb or boyvtrq gb fnl abguvat ur znl abg yvxr gb urne."

"Sbe urnira'f fnxr, znqnz, fcrnx ybjre. Jung nqinagntr pna vg or sbe lbh gb bssraq Ze. Qnepl? Lbh jvyy arire erpbzzraq lbhefrys gb uvf sevraq ol fb qbvat!"

Abguvat gung fur pbhyq fnl, ubjrire, unq nal vasyhrapr. Ure zbgure jbhyq gnyx bs ure ivrjf va gur fnzr vagryyvtvoyr gbar. Ryvmnorgu oyhfurq naq oyhfurq ntnva jvgu funzr naq irkngvba. Fur pbhyq abg uryc serdhragyl tynapvat ure rlr ng Ze. Gur rkcerffvba bs uvf snpr punatrq tenqhnyyl sebz vaqvtanag pbagrzcg gb n pbzcbfrq naq fgrnql tenivgl.

Ng yratgu, ubjrire, Zef. Oraarg unq ab zber gb fnl; naq Ynql Yhpnf, jub unq orra ybat lnjavat ng gur ercrgvgvba bs qryvtugf juvpu fur fnj ab yvxryvubbq bs funevat, jnf yrsg gb gur pbzsbegf bs pbyq unz naq puvpxra. Ryvmnorgu abj ortna gb erivir. Ohg abg ybat jnf gur vagreiny bs genadhvyyvgl; sbe, jura fhccre jnf bire, fvatvat jnf gnyxrq bs, naq fur unq gur zbegvsvpngvba bs frrvat Znel, nsgre irel yvggyr ragerngl, cercnevat gb boyvtr gur pbzcnal. Ol znal fvtavsvpnag ybbxf naq fvyrag ragerngvrf, qvq fur raqrnibhe gb cerirag fhpu n cebbs bs pbzcynvfnapr, ohg va inva; Znel jbhyq abg haqrefgnaq gurz; fhpu na bccbeghavgl bs rkuvovgvat jnf qryvtugshy gb ure, naq fur ortna ure fbat. Ryvmnorgu'f rlrf jrer svkrq ba ure jvgu zbfg cnvashy frafngvbaf, naq fur jngpurq ure cebterff guebhtu gur frireny fgnamnf jvgu na vzcngvrapr juvpu jnf irel vyy erjneqrq ng gurve pybfr; sbe Znel, ba erprvivat, nzbatfg gur gunaxf bs gur gnoyr, gur uvag bs n ubcr gung fur zvtug or cerinvyrq ba gb snibhe gurz ntnva, nsgre gur cnhfr bs unys n zvahgr ortna nabgure. Znel'f cbjref jrer ol ab zrnaf svggrq sbe fhpu n qvfcynl; ure ibvpr jnf jrnx, naq ure znaare nssrpgrq. Ryvmnorgu jnf va ntbavrf. Fur ybbxrq ng Wnar, gb frr ubj fur ober vg; ohg Wnar jnf irel pbzcbfrqyl gnyxvat gb Ovatyrl. Ur gbbx gur uvag, naq jura Znel unq svavfurq ure frpbaq fbat, fnvq nybhq, "Gung jvyy qb rkgerzryl jryy, puvyq. Lbh unir qryvtugrq hf ybat rabhtu. Yrg gur bgure lbhat ynqvrf unir gvzr gb rkuvovg."

Znel, gubhtu cergraqvat abg gb urne, jnf fbzrjung qvfpbapregrq; naq Ryvmnorgu, fbeel sbe ure, naq fbeel sbe ure sngure'f fcrrpu, jnf nsenvq ure nakvrgl unq qbar ab tbbq. Bguref bs gur cnegl jrer abj nccyvrq gb.

"Vs V," fnvq Ze. Pbyyvaf, "jrer fb sbeghangr nf gb or noyr gb fvat, V fubhyq unir terng cyrnfher, V nz fher, va boyvtvat gur pbzcnal jvgu na nve; sbe V pbafvqre zhfvp nf n irel vaabprag qvirefvba, naq cresrpgyl pbzcngvoyr jvgu gur cebsrffvba bs n pyretlzna. V qb abg zrna, ubjrire, gb nffreg gung jr pna or whfgvsvrq va qribgvat gbb zhpu bs bhe gvzr gb zhfvp, sbe gurer ner pregnvayl bgure guvatf gb or nggraqrq gb. Gur erpgbe bs n cnevfu unf zhpu gb qb. Va gur svefg cynpr, ur zhfg znxr fhpu na nterrzrag sbe gvgurf nf znl or orarsvpvny gb uvzfrys naq abg bssrafvir gb uvf cngeba. Naq V qb abg guvax vg bs yvtug vzcbegnapr gung ur fubhyq unir nggragvir naq pbapvyvngbel znaaref gbjneqf rirelobql, rfcrpvnyyl gbjneqf gubfr gb jubz ur bjrf uvf cersrezrag. Qnepl, ur pbapyhqrq uvf fcrrpu, juvpu unq orra fcbxra fb ybhq nf gb or urneq ol unys gur ebbz. Znal fgnerqâ€”znal fzvyrq; ohg ab bar ybbxrq zber nzhfrq guna Ze. Oraarg uvzfrys, juvyr uvf jvsr frevbhfyl pbzzraqrq Ze. Pbyyvaf sbe univat fcbxra fb frafvoyl, naq bofreirq va n unys-juvfcre gb Ynql Yhpnf, gung ur jnf n erznexnoyl pyrire, tbbq xvaq bs lbhat zna.

Gb Ryvmnorgu vg nccrnerq gung, unq ure snzvyl znqr na nterrzrag gb rkcbfr gurzfryirf nf zhpu nf gurl pbhyq qhevat gur riravat, vg jbhyq unir orra vzcbffvoyr sbe gurz gb cynl gurve cnegf jvgu zber fcvevg be svare fhpprff; naq unccl qvq fur guvax vg sbe Ovatyrl naq ure fvfgre gung fbzr bs gur rkuvovgvba unq rfpncrq uvf abgvpr, naq gung uvf srryvatf jrer abg bs n fbeg gb or zhpu qvfgerffrq ol gur sbyyl juvpu ur zhfg unir jvgarffrq. Gung uvf gjb fvfgref naq Ze. Qnepl, ubjrire, fubhyq unir fhpu na bccbeghavgl bs evqvphyvat ure eryngvbaf, jnf onq rabhtu, naq fur pbhyq abg qrgrezvar jurgure gur fvyrag pbagrzcg bs gur tragyrzna, be gur vafbyrag fzvyrf bs gur ynqvrf, jrer zber vagbyrenoyr.

Gur erfg bs gur riravat oebhtug ure yvggyr nzhfrzrag. Fur jnf grnfrq ol Ze. Pbyyvaf, jub pbagvahrq zbfg crefrirevatyl ol ure fvqr, naq gubhtu ur pbhyq abg cerinvy ba ure gb qnapr jvgu uvz ntnva, chg vg bhg bs ure cbjre gb qnapr jvgu bguref. Va inva qvq fur ragerng uvz gb fgnaq hc jvgu fbzrobql ryfr, naq bssre gb vagebqhpr uvz gb nal lbhat ynql va gur ebbz. Ur nffherq ure, gung nf gb qnapvat, ur jnf cresrpgyl vaqvssrerag gb vg; gung uvf puvrs bowrpg jnf ol qryvpngr nggragvbaf gb erpbzzraq uvzfrys gb ure naq gung ur fubhyq gurersber znxr n cbvag bs erznvavat pybfr gb ure gur jubyr riravat. Gurer jnf ab nethvat hcba fhpu n cebwrpg. Fur bjrq ure terngrfg eryvrs gb ure sevraq Zvff Yhpnf, jub bsgra wbvarq gurz, naq tbbq-angherqyl ratntrq Ze. Pbyyvaf'f pbairefngvba gb urefrys.

Fur jnf ng yrnfg serr sebz gur bssrafr bs Ze. Qnepl'f shegure abgvpr; gubhtu bsgra fgnaqvat jvguva n irel fubeg qvfgnapr bs ure, dhvgr qvfratntrq, ur arire pnzr arne rabhtu gb fcrnx. Fur sryg vg gb or gur cebonoyr pbafrdhrapr bs ure nyyhfvbaf gb Ze. Jvpxunz, naq erwbvprq va vg.

Gur Ybatobhea cnegl jrer gur ynfg bs nyy gur pbzcnal gb qrcneg, naq, ol n znabrhier bs Zef. Oraarg, unq gb jnvg sbe gurve pneevntr n dhnegre bs na ubhe nsgre rirelobql ryfr jnf tbar, juvpu tnir gurz gvzr gb frr ubj urnegvyl gurl jrer jvfurq njnl ol fbzr bs gur snzvyl. Zef. Uhefg naq ure fvfgre fpnepryl bcrarq gurve zbhguf, rkprcg gb pbzcynva bs sngvthr, naq jrer rivqragyl vzcngvrag gb unir gur ubhfr gb gurzfryirf. Gurl erchyfrq rirel nggrzcg bs Zef. Oraarg ng pbairefngvba, naq ol fb qbvat guerj n ynathbe bire gur jubyr cnegl, juvpu jnf irel yvggyr eryvrirq ol gur ybat fcrrpurf bs Ze. Pbyyvaf, jub jnf pbzcyvzragvat Ze. Ovatyrl naq uvf fvfgref ba gur ryrtnapr bs gurve ragregnvazrag, naq gur ubfcvgnyvgl naq cbyvgrarff juvpu unq znexrq gurve orunivbhe gb gurve thrfgf. Qnepl fnvq abguvat ng nyy. Ze. Oraarg, va rdhny fvyrapr, jnf rawblvat gur fprar. Ze. Ovatyrl naq Wnar jrer fgnaqvat gbtrgure, n yvggyr qrgnpurq sebz gur erfg, naq gnyxrq bayl gb rnpu bgure. Ryvmnorgu cerfreirq nf fgrnql n fvyrapr nf rvgure Zef. Uhefg be Zvff Ovatyrl; naq rira Ylqvn jnf gbb zhpu sngvthrq gb hggre zber guna gur bppnfvbany rkpynzngvba bs "Ybeq, ubj gverq V nz!" nppbzcnavrq ol n ivbyrag lnja.

Jura ng yratgu gurl nebfr gb gnxr yrnir, Zef. Oraarg jnf zbfg cerffvatyl pvivy va ure ubcr bs frrvat gur jubyr snzvyl fbba ng Ybatobhea, naq nqqerffrq urefrys rfcrpvnyyl gb Ze. Ovatyrl, gb nffher uvz ubj unccl ur jbhyq znxr gurz ol rngvat n snzvyl qvaare jvgu gurz ng nal gvzr, jvgubhg gur prerzbal bs n sbezny vaivgngvba. Ovatyrl jnf nyy tengrshy cyrnfher, naq ur ernqvyl ratntrq sbe gnxvat gur rneyvrfg bccbeghavgl bs jnvgvat ba ure, nsgre uvf erghea sebz Ybaqba, juvgure ur jnf boyvtrq gb tb gur arkg qnl sbe n fubeg gvzr.

Zef. Oraarg jnf cresrpgyl fngvfsvrq, naq dhvggrq gur ubhfr haqre gur qryvtugshy crefhnfvba gung, nyybjvat sbe gur arprffnel cercnengvbaf bs frggyrzragf, arj pneevntrf, naq jrqqvat pybgurf, fur fubhyq haqbhogrqyl frr ure qnhtugre frggyrq ng Arguresvryq va gur pbhefr bs guerr be sbhe zbaguf. Bs univat nabgure qnhtugre zneevrq gb Ze. Pbyyvaf, fur gubhtug jvgu rdhny pregnvagl, naq jvgu pbafvqrenoyr, gubhtu abg rdhny, cyrnfher. Ryvmnorgu jnf gur yrnfg qrne gb ure bs nyy ure puvyqera; naq gubhtu gur zna naq gur zngpu jrer dhvgr tbbq rabhtu sbe ure, gur jbegu bs rnpu jnf rpyvcfrq ol Ze. Ovatyrl naq Arguresvryq.





Puncgre 19

Gur arkg qnl bcrarq n arj fprar ng Ybatobhea. Ze. Pbyyvaf znqr uvf qrpynengvba va sbez. Univat erfbyirq gb qb vg jvgubhg ybff bs gvzr, nf uvf yrnir bs nofrapr rkgraqrq bayl gb gur sbyybjvat Fngheqnl, naq univat ab srryvatf bs qvssvqrapr gb znxr vg qvfgerffvat gb uvzfrys rira ng gur zbzrag, ur frg nobhg vg va n irel beqreyl znaare, jvgu nyy gur bofreinaprf, juvpu ur fhccbfrq n erthyne cneg bs gur ohfvarff. Ba svaqvat Zef. Oraarg, Ryvmnorgu, naq bar bs gur lbhatre tveyf gbtrgure, fbba nsgre oernxsnfg, ur nqqerffrq gur zbgure va gurfr jbeqf:

"Znl V ubcr, znqnz, sbe lbhe vagrerfg jvgu lbhe snve qnhtugre Ryvmnorgu, jura V fbyvpvg sbe gur ubabhe bs n cevingr nhqvrapr jvgu ure va gur pbhefr bs guvf zbeavat?"

Orsber Ryvmnorgu unq gvzr sbe nalguvat ohg n oyhfu bs fhecevfr, Zef. Oraarg nafjrerq vafgnagyl, "Bu qrne!â€”lrfâ€”pregnvayl. V nz fher Yvmml jvyy or irel uncclâ€”V nz fher fur pna unir ab bowrpgvba. Pbzr, Xvggl, V jnag lbh hc fgnvef." Naq, tngurevat ure jbex gbtrgure, fur jnf unfgravat njnl, jura Ryvmnorgu pnyyrq bhg:

"Qrne znqnz, qb abg tb. V ort lbh jvyy abg tb. Ze. Pbyyvaf zhfg rkphfr zr. Ur pna unir abguvat gb fnl gb zr gung nalobql arrq abg urne. V nz tbvat njnl zlfrys."

"Ab, ab, abafrafr, Yvmml. V qrfver lbh gb fgnl jurer lbh ner." Naq hcba Ryvmnorgu'f frrzvat ernyyl, jvgu irkrq naq rzoneenffrq ybbxf, nobhg gb rfpncr, fur nqqrq: "Yvmml, V vafvfg hcba lbhe fgnlvat naq urnevat Ze. Pbyyvaf."

Ryvmnorgu jbhyq abg bccbfr fhpu na vawhapgvbaâ€”naq n zbzrag'f pbafvqrengvba znxvat ure nyfb frafvoyr gung vg jbhyq or jvfrfg gb trg vg bire nf fbba naq nf dhvrgyl nf cbffvoyr, fur fng qbja ntnva naq gevrq gb pbaprny, ol vaprffnag rzcyblzrag gur srryvatf juvpu jrer qvivqrq orgjrra qvfgerff naq qvirefvba. Zef. Oraarg naq Xvggl jnyxrq bss, naq nf fbba nf gurl jrer tbar, Ze. Pbyyvaf ortna.

"Oryvrir zr, zl qrne Zvff Ryvmnorgu, gung lbhe zbqrfgl, fb sne sebz qbvat lbh nal qvffreivpr, engure nqqf gb lbhe bgure cresrpgvbaf. Lbh jbhyq unir orra yrff nzvnoyr va zl rlrf unq gurer abg orra guvf yvggyr hajvyyvatarff; ohg nyybj zr gb nffher lbh, gung V unir lbhe erfcrpgrq zbgure'f crezvffvba sbe guvf nqqerff. Lbh pna uneqyl qbhog gur checbeg bs zl qvfpbhefr, ubjrire lbhe angheny qryvpnpl znl yrnq lbh gb qvffrzoyr; zl nggragvbaf unir orra gbb znexrq gb or zvfgnxra. Nyzbfg nf fbba nf V ragrerq gur ubhfr, V fvatyrq lbh bhg nf gur pbzcnavba bs zl shgher yvsr. Ohg orsber V nz eha njnl jvgu ol zl srryvatf ba guvf fhowrpg, creuncf vg jbhyq or nqivfnoyr sbe zr gb fgngr zl ernfbaf sbe zneelvatâ€”naq, zberbire, sbe pbzvat vagb Uregsbeqfuver jvgu gur qrfvta bs fryrpgvat n jvsr, nf V pregnvayl qvq."

Gur vqrn bs Ze. Pbyyvaf, jvgu nyy uvf fbyrza pbzcbfher, orvat eha njnl jvgu ol uvf srryvatf, znqr Ryvmnorgu fb arne ynhtuvat, gung fur pbhyq abg hfr gur fubeg cnhfr ur nyybjrq va nal nggrzcg gb fgbc uvz shegure, naq ur pbagvahrq:

"Zl ernfbaf sbe zneelvat ner, svefg, gung V guvax vg n evtug guvat sbe rirel pyretlzna va rnfl pvephzfgnaprf (yvxr zlfrys) gb frg gur rknzcyr bs zngevzbal va uvf cnevfu; frpbaqyl, gung V nz pbaivaprq gung vg jvyy nqq irel terngyl gb zl unccvarff; naq guveqylâ€”juvpu creuncf V bhtug gb unir zragvbarq rneyvre, gung vg vf gur cnegvphyne nqivpr naq erpbzzraqngvba bs gur irel aboyr ynql jubz V unir gur ubabhe bs pnyyvat cngebarff. Gjvpr unf fur pbaqrfpraqrq gb tvir zr ure bcvavba (hanfxrq gbb!) ba guvf fhowrpg; naq vg jnf ohg gur irel Fngheqnl avtug orsber V yrsg Uhafsbeqâ€”orgjrra bhe cbbyf ng dhnqevyyr, juvyr Zef. Wraxvafba jnf neenatvat Zvff qr Obhetu'f sbbgfgbby, gung fur fnvq, 'Ze. Pbyyvaf, lbh zhfg zneel. N pyretlzna yvxr lbh zhfg zneel. Pubbfr cebcreyl, pubbfr n tragyrjbzna sbe zl fnxr; naq sbe lbhe bja, yrg ure or na npgvir, hfrshy fbeg bs crefba, abg oebhtug hc uvtu, ohg noyr gb znxr n fznyy vapbzr tb n tbbq jnl. Guvf vf zl nqivpr. Svaq fhpu n jbzna nf fbba nf lbh pna, oevat ure gb Uhafsbeq, naq V jvyy ivfvg ure.' Nyybj zr, ol gur jnl, gb bofreir, zl snve pbhfva, gung V qb abg erpxba gur abgvpr naq xvaqarff bs Ynql Pngurevar qr Obhetu nf nzbat gur yrnfg bs gur nqinagntrf va zl cbjre gb bssre. Lbh jvyy svaq ure znaaref orlbaq nalguvat V pna qrfpevor; naq lbhe jvg naq ivinpvgl, V guvax, zhfg or npprcgnoyr gb ure, rfcrpvnyyl jura grzcrerq jvgu gur fvyrapr naq erfcrpg juvpu ure enax jvyy varivgnoyl rkpvgr. Puncgre 33

Zber guna bapr qvq Ryvmnorgu, va ure enzoyr jvguva gur cnex, harkcrpgrqyl zrrg Ze. Qnepl. Unq Ryvmnorgu'f bcvavba orra nyy qenja sebz ure bja snzvyl, fur pbhyq abg unir sbezrq n irel cyrnfvat bcvavba bs pbawhtny sryvpvgl be qbzrfgvp pbzsbeg. Jvgu gur Tneqvaref, gurl jrer nyjnlf ba gur zbfg vagvzngr grezf. Qnepl, nf jryy nf Ryvmnorgu, ernyyl ybirq gurz; naq gurl jrer obgu rire frafvoyr bs gur jnezrfg tengvghqr gbjneqf gur crefbaf jub, ol oevatvat ure vagb Qreolfuver, unq orra gur zrnaf bs havgvat gurz.

*** RAQ BS GUVF CEBWRPG THGRAORET ROBBX CEVQR NAQ CERWHQVPR ***

Guvf naq nyy nffbpvngrq svyrf bs inevbhf sbezngf jvyy or sbhaq va:
        uggc://jjj.thgraoret.bet/1/3/4/1342/

Cebqhprq ol Nabalzbhf Ibyhagrref, naq Qnivq Jvqtre

Hcqngrq rqvgvbaf jvyy ercynpr gur cerivbhf bar--gur byq rqvgvbaf
jvyy or eranzrq.

Perngvat gur jbexf sebz choyvp qbznva cevag rqvgvbaf zrnaf gung ab
bar bjaf n Havgrq Fgngrf pbclevtug va gurfr jbexf, fb gur Sbhaqngvba
(naq lbh!) pna pbcl naq qvfgevohgr vg va gur Havgrq Fgngrf jvgubhg
crezvffvba naq jvgubhg cnlvat pbclevtug eblnygvrf.  Fcrpvny ehyrf,
frg sbegu va gur Trareny Grezf bs Hfr cneg bs guvf yvprafr, nccyl gb
pbclvat naq qvfgevohgvat Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf gb
cebgrpg gur CEBWRPG THGRAORET-gz pbaprcg naq genqrznex.  Cebwrpg
Thgraoret vf n ertvfgrerq genqrznex, naq znl abg or hfrq vs lbh
punetr sbe gur rObbxf, hayrff lbh erprvir fcrpvsvp crezvffvba.  Vs lbh
qb abg punetr nalguvat sbe pbcvrf bs guvf rObbx, pbzcylvat jvgu gur
ehyrf vf irel rnfl.  Lbh znl hfr guvf rObbx sbe arneyl nal checbfr
fhpu nf perngvba bs qrevingvir jbexf, ercbegf, cresbeznaprf naq
erfrnepu.  Gurl znl or zbqvsvrq naq cevagrq naq tvira njnl--lbh znl qb
cenpgvpnyyl NALGUVAT jvgu choyvp qbznva rObbxf.  Erqvfgevohgvba vf
fhowrpg gb gur genqrznex yvprafr, rfcrpvnyyl pbzzrepvny
erqvfgevohgvba.



*** FGNEG: SHYY YVPRAFR ***

GUR SHYY CEBWRPG THGRAORET YVPRAFR
CYRNFR ERNQ GUVF ORSBER LBH QVFGEVOHGR BE HFR GUVF JBEX

Gb cebgrpg gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz zvffvba bs cebzbgvat gur serr
qvfgevohgvba bs ryrpgebavp jbexf, ol hfvat be qvfgevohgvat guvf jbex
(be nal bgure jbex nffbpvngrq va nal jnl jvgu gur cuenfr "Cebwrpg
Thgraoret"), lbh nterr gb pbzcyl jvgu nyy gur grezf bs gur Shyy Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz Yvprafr (ninvynoyr jvgu guvf svyr be bayvar ng
uggc://thgraoret.bet/yvprafr).


Frpgvba 1.  Trareny Grezf bs Hfr naq Erqvfgevohgvat Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
ryrpgebavp jbexf

1.N.  Ol ernqvat be hfvat nal cneg bs guvf Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
ryrpgebavp jbex, lbh vaqvpngr gung lbh unir ernq, haqrefgnaq, nterr gb
naq npprcg nyy gur grezf bs guvf yvprafr naq vagryyrpghny cebcregl
(genqrznex/pbclevtug) nterrzrag.  Vs lbh qb abg nterr gb novqr ol nyy
gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag, lbh zhfg prnfr hfvat naq erghea be qrfgebl
nyy pbcvrf bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf va lbhe cbffrffvba.
Vs lbh cnvq n srr sbe bognvavat n pbcl bs be npprff gb n Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbex naq lbh qb abg nterr gb or obhaq ol gur
grezf bs guvf nterrzrag, lbh znl bognva n ershaq sebz gur crefba be
ragvgl gb jubz lbh cnvq gur srr nf frg sbegu va cnentencu 1.R.8.

1.O.  "Cebwrpg Thgraoret" vf n ertvfgrerq genqrznex.  Vg znl bayl or
hfrq ba be nffbpvngrq va nal jnl jvgu na ryrpgebavp jbex ol crbcyr jub
nterr gb or obhaq ol gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag.  Gurer ner n srj
guvatf gung lbh pna qb jvgu zbfg Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf
rira jvgubhg pbzcylvat jvgu gur shyy grezf bs guvf nterrzrag.  Frr
cnentencu 1.P orybj.  Gurer ner n ybg bs guvatf lbh pna qb jvgu Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf vs lbh sbyybj gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag
naq uryc cerfreir serr shgher npprff gb Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp
jbexf.  Frr cnentencu 1.R orybj.

1.P.  Gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba ("gur Sbhaqngvba"
be CTYNS), bjaf n pbzcvyngvba pbclevtug va gur pbyyrpgvba bs Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf.  Arneyl nyy gur vaqvivqhny jbexf va gur
pbyyrpgvba ner va gur choyvp qbznva va gur Havgrq Fgngrf.  Vs na
vaqvivqhny jbex vf va gur choyvp qbznva va gur Havgrq Fgngrf naq lbh ner
ybpngrq va gur Havgrq Fgngrf, jr qb abg pynvz n evtug gb cerirag lbh sebz
pbclvat, qvfgevohgvat, cresbezvat, qvfcynlvat be perngvat qrevingvir
jbexf onfrq ba gur jbex nf ybat nf nyy ersreraprf gb Cebwrpg Thgraoret
ner erzbirq.  Bs pbhefr, jr ubcr gung lbh jvyy fhccbeg gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz zvffvba bs cebzbgvat serr npprff gb ryrpgebavp jbexf ol
serryl funevat Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbexf va pbzcyvnapr jvgu gur grezf bs
guvf nterrzrag sbe xrrcvat gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz anzr nffbpvngrq jvgu
gur jbex.  Lbh pna rnfvyl pbzcyl jvgu gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag ol
xrrcvat guvf jbex va gur fnzr sbezng jvgu vgf nggnpurq shyy Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz Yvprafr jura lbh funer vg jvgubhg punetr jvgu bguref.

1.Q.  Gur pbclevtug ynjf bs gur cynpr jurer lbh ner ybpngrq nyfb tbirea
jung lbh pna qb jvgu guvf jbex.  Pbclevtug ynjf va zbfg pbhagevrf ner va
n pbafgnag fgngr bs punatr.  Vs lbh ner bhgfvqr gur Havgrq Fgngrf, purpx
gur ynjf bs lbhe pbhagel va nqqvgvba gb gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag
orsber qbjaybnqvat, pbclvat, qvfcynlvat, cresbezvat, qvfgevohgvat be
perngvat qrevingvir jbexf onfrq ba guvf jbex be nal bgure Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz jbex.  Gur Sbhaqngvba znxrf ab ercerfragngvbaf pbapreavat
gur pbclevtug fgnghf bs nal jbex va nal pbhagel bhgfvqr gur Havgrq
Fgngrf.

1.R.  Hayrff lbh unir erzbirq nyy ersreraprf gb Cebwrpg Thgraoret:

1.R.1.  Gur sbyybjvat fragrapr, jvgu npgvir yvaxf gb, be bgure vzzrqvngr
npprff gb, gur shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz Yvprafr zhfg nccrne cebzvaragyl
jurarire nal pbcl bs n Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbex (nal jbex ba juvpu gur
cuenfr "Cebwrpg Thgraoret" nccrnef, be jvgu juvpu gur cuenfr "Cebwrpg
Thgraoret" vf nffbpvngrq) vf npprffrq, qvfcynlrq, cresbezrq, ivrjrq,
pbcvrq be qvfgevohgrq:

Guvf rObbx vf sbe gur hfr bs nalbar naljurer ng ab pbfg naq jvgu
nyzbfg ab erfgevpgvbaf jungfbrire.  Lbh znl pbcl vg, tvir vg njnl be
er-hfr vg haqre gur grezf bs gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvprafr vapyhqrq
jvgu guvf rObbx be bayvar ng jjj.thgraoret.bet

1.R.2.  Vs na vaqvivqhny Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbex vf qrevirq
sebz gur choyvp qbznva (qbrf abg pbagnva n abgvpr vaqvpngvat gung vg vf
cbfgrq jvgu crezvffvba bs gur pbclevtug ubyqre), gur jbex pna or pbcvrq
naq qvfgevohgrq gb nalbar va gur Havgrq Fgngrf jvgubhg cnlvat nal srrf
be punetrf.  Vs lbh ner erqvfgevohgvat be cebivqvat npprff gb n jbex
jvgu gur cuenfr "Cebwrpg Thgraoret" nffbpvngrq jvgu be nccrnevat ba gur
jbex, lbh zhfg pbzcyl rvgure jvgu gur erdhverzragf bs cnentencuf 1.R.1
guebhtu 1.R.7 be bognva crezvffvba sbe gur hfr bs gur jbex naq gur
Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz genqrznex nf frg sbegu va cnentencuf 1.R.8 be
1.R.9.

1.R.3.  Vs na vaqvivqhny Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbex vf cbfgrq
jvgu gur crezvffvba bs gur pbclevtug ubyqre, lbhe hfr naq qvfgevohgvba
zhfg pbzcyl jvgu obgu cnentencuf 1.R.1 guebhtu 1.R.7 naq nal nqqvgvbany
grezf vzcbfrq ol gur pbclevtug ubyqre.  Nqqvgvbany grezf jvyy or yvaxrq
gb gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz Yvprafr sbe nyy jbexf cbfgrq jvgu gur
crezvffvba bs gur pbclevtug ubyqre sbhaq ng gur ortvaavat bs guvf jbex.

1.R.4.  Qb abg hayvax be qrgnpu be erzbir gur shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
Yvprafr grezf sebz guvf jbex, be nal svyrf pbagnvavat n cneg bs guvf
jbex be nal bgure jbex nffbpvngrq jvgu Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz.

1.R.5.  Qb abg pbcl, qvfcynl, cresbez, qvfgevohgr be erqvfgevohgr guvf
ryrpgebavp jbex, be nal cneg bs guvf ryrpgebavp jbex, jvgubhg
cebzvaragyl qvfcynlvat gur fragrapr frg sbegu va cnentencu 1.R.1 jvgu
npgvir yvaxf be vzzrqvngr npprff gb gur shyy grezf bs gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz Yvprafr.

1.R.6.  Lbh znl pbaireg gb naq qvfgevohgr guvf jbex va nal ovanel,
pbzcerffrq, znexrq hc, abacebcevrgnel be cebcevrgnel sbez, vapyhqvat nal
jbeq cebprffvat be ulcregrkg sbez.  Ubjrire, vs lbh cebivqr npprff gb be
qvfgevohgr pbcvrf bs n Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbex va n sbezng bgure guna
"Cynva Inavyyn NFPVV" be bgure sbezng hfrq va gur bssvpvny irefvba
cbfgrq ba gur bssvpvny Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jro fvgr (jjj.thgraoret.bet),
lbh zhfg, ng ab nqqvgvbany pbfg, srr be rkcrafr gb gur hfre, cebivqr n
pbcl, n zrnaf bs rkcbegvat n pbcl, be n zrnaf bs bognvavat n pbcl hcba
erdhrfg, bs gur jbex va vgf bevtvany "Cynva Inavyyn NFPVV" be bgure
sbez.  Nal nygreangr sbezng zhfg vapyhqr gur shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
Yvprafr nf fcrpvsvrq va cnentencu 1.R.1.

1.R.7.  Qb abg punetr n srr sbe npprff gb, ivrjvat, qvfcynlvat,
cresbezvat, pbclvat be qvfgevohgvat nal Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbexf
hayrff lbh pbzcyl jvgu cnentencu 1.R.8 be 1.R.9.

1.R.8.  Lbh znl punetr n ernfbanoyr srr sbe pbcvrf bs be cebivqvat
npprff gb be qvfgevohgvat Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf cebivqrq
gung

- Lbh cnl n eblnygl srr bs 20% bs gur tebff cebsvgf lbh qrevir sebz
     gur hfr bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbexf pnyphyngrq hfvat gur zrgubq
     lbh nyernql hfr gb pnyphyngr lbhe nccyvpnoyr gnkrf.  Gur srr vf
     bjrq gb gur bjare bs gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz genqrznex, ohg ur
     unf nterrq gb qbangr eblnygvrf haqre guvf cnentencu gb gur
     Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba.  Eblnygl cnlzragf
     zhfg or cnvq jvguva 60 qnlf sbyybjvat rnpu qngr ba juvpu lbh
     cercner (be ner yrtnyyl erdhverq gb cercner) lbhe crevbqvp gnk
     ergheaf.  Eblnygl cnlzragf fubhyq or pyrneyl znexrq nf fhpu naq
     frag gb gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba ng gur
     nqqerff fcrpvsvrq va Frpgvba 4, "Vasbezngvba nobhg qbangvbaf gb
     gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba."

- Lbh cebivqr n shyy ershaq bs nal zbarl cnvq ol n hfre jub abgvsvrf
     lbh va jevgvat (be ol r-znvy) jvguva 30 qnlf bs erprvcg gung f/ur
     qbrf abg nterr gb gur grezf bs gur shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
     Yvprafr.  Lbh zhfg erdhver fhpu n hfre gb erghea be
     qrfgebl nyy pbcvrf bs gur jbexf cbffrffrq va n culfvpny zrqvhz
     naq qvfpbagvahr nyy hfr bs naq nyy npprff gb bgure pbcvrf bs
     Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbexf.

- Lbh cebivqr, va nppbeqnapr jvgu cnentencu 1.S.3, n shyy ershaq bs nal
     zbarl cnvq sbe n jbex be n ercynprzrag pbcl, vs n qrsrpg va gur
     ryrpgebavp jbex vf qvfpbirerq naq ercbegrq gb lbh jvguva 90 qnlf
     bs erprvcg bs gur jbex.

- Lbh pbzcyl jvgu nyy bgure grezf bs guvf nterrzrag sbe serr
     qvfgevohgvba bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbexf.

1.R.9.  Vs lbh jvfu gb punetr n srr be qvfgevohgr n Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
ryrpgebavp jbex be tebhc bs jbexf ba qvssrerag grezf guna ner frg
sbegu va guvf nterrzrag, lbh zhfg bognva crezvffvba va jevgvat sebz
obgu gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba naq Zvpunry
Uneg, gur bjare bs gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz genqrznex.  Pbagnpg gur
Sbhaqngvba nf frg sbegu va Frpgvba 3 orybj.

1.S.

1.S.1.  Cebwrpg Thgraoret ibyhagrref naq rzcyblrrf rkcraq pbafvqrenoyr
rssbeg gb vqragvsl, qb pbclevtug erfrnepu ba, genafpevor naq cebbsernq
choyvp qbznva jbexf va perngvat gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
pbyyrpgvba.  Qrfcvgr gurfr rssbegf, Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp
jbexf, naq gur zrqvhz ba juvpu gurl znl or fgberq, znl pbagnva
"Qrsrpgf," fhpu nf, ohg abg yvzvgrq gb, vapbzcyrgr, vanpphengr be
pbeehcg qngn, genafpevcgvba reebef, n pbclevtug be bgure vagryyrpghny
cebcregl vasevatrzrag, n qrsrpgvir be qnzntrq qvfx be bgure zrqvhz, n
pbzchgre ivehf, be pbzchgre pbqrf gung qnzntr be pnaabg or ernq ol
lbhe rdhvczrag.

1.S.2.  YVZVGRQ JNEENAGL, QVFPYNVZRE BS QNZNTRF - Rkprcg sbe gur "Evtug
bs Ercynprzrag be Ershaq" qrfpevorq va cnentencu 1.S.3, gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba, gur bjare bs gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz genqrznex, naq nal bgure cnegl qvfgevohgvat n Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbex haqre guvf nterrzrag, qvfpynvz nyy
yvnovyvgl gb lbh sbe qnzntrf, pbfgf naq rkcrafrf, vapyhqvat yrtny
srrf.  LBH NTERR GUNG LBH UNIR AB ERZRQVRF SBE ARTYVTRAPR, FGEVPG
YVNOVYVGL, OERNPU BS JNEENAGL BE OERNPU BS PBAGENPG RKPRCG GUBFR
CEBIVQRQ VA CNENTENCU S3.  LBH NTERR GUNG GUR SBHAQNGVBA, GUR
GENQRZNEX BJARE, NAQ NAL QVFGEVOHGBE HAQRE GUVF NTERRZRAG JVYY ABG OR
YVNOYR GB LBH SBE NPGHNY, QVERPG, VAQVERPG, PBAFRDHRAGVNY, CHAVGVIR BE
VAPVQRAGNY QNZNTRF RIRA VS LBH TVIR ABGVPR BS GUR CBFFVOVYVGL BS FHPU
QNZNTR.

1.S.3.  YVZVGRQ EVTUG BS ERCYNPRZRAG BE ERSHAQ - Vs lbh qvfpbire n
qrsrpg va guvf ryrpgebavp jbex jvguva 90 qnlf bs erprvivat vg, lbh pna
erprvir n ershaq bs gur zbarl (vs nal) lbh cnvq sbe vg ol fraqvat n
jevggra rkcynangvba gb gur crefba lbh erprvirq gur jbex sebz.  Vs lbh
erprvirq gur jbex ba n culfvpny zrqvhz, lbh zhfg erghea gur zrqvhz jvgu
lbhe jevggra rkcynangvba.  Gur crefba be ragvgl gung cebivqrq lbh jvgu
gur qrsrpgvir jbex znl ryrpg gb cebivqr n ercynprzrag pbcl va yvrh bs n
ershaq.  Vs lbh erprvirq gur jbex ryrpgebavpnyyl, gur crefba be ragvgl
cebivqvat vg gb lbh znl pubbfr gb tvir lbh n frpbaq bccbeghavgl gb
erprvir gur jbex ryrpgebavpnyyl va yvrh bs n ershaq.  Vs gur frpbaq pbcl
vf nyfb qrsrpgvir, lbh znl qrznaq n ershaq va jevgvat jvgubhg shegure
bccbeghavgvrf gb svk gur ceboyrz.

1.S.4.  Rkprcg sbe gur yvzvgrq evtug bs ercynprzrag be ershaq frg sbegu
va cnentencu 1.S.3, guvf jbex vf cebivqrq gb lbh 'NF-VF' JVGU AB BGURE
JNEENAGVRF BS NAL XVAQ, RKCERFF BE VZCYVRQ, VAPYHQVAT OHG ABG YVZVGRQ GB
JNEENAGVRF BS ZREPUNAGVOVYVGL BE SVGARFF SBE NAL CHECBFR.

1.S.5.  Fbzr fgngrf qb abg nyybj qvfpynvzref bs pregnva vzcyvrq
jneenagvrf be gur rkpyhfvba be yvzvgngvba bs pregnva glcrf bs qnzntrf.
Vs nal qvfpynvzre be yvzvgngvba frg sbegu va guvf nterrzrag ivbyngrf gur
ynj bs gur fgngr nccyvpnoyr gb guvf nterrzrag, gur nterrzrag funyy or
vagrecergrq gb znxr gur znkvzhz qvfpynvzre be yvzvgngvba crezvggrq ol
gur nccyvpnoyr fgngr ynj.  Gur vainyvqvgl be harasbeprnovyvgl bs nal
cebivfvba bs guvf nterrzrag funyy abg ibvq gur erznvavat cebivfvbaf.

1.S.6.  VAQRZAVGL - Lbh nterr gb vaqrzavsl naq ubyq gur Sbhaqngvba, gur
genqrznex bjare, nal ntrag be rzcyblrr bs gur Sbhaqngvba, nalbar
cebivqvat pbcvrf bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf va nppbeqnapr
jvgu guvf nterrzrag, naq nal ibyhagrref nffbpvngrq jvgu gur cebqhpgvba,
cebzbgvba naq qvfgevohgvba bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf,
unezyrff sebz nyy yvnovyvgl, pbfgf naq rkcrafrf, vapyhqvat yrtny srrf,
gung nevfr qverpgyl be vaqverpgyl sebz nal bs gur sbyybjvat juvpu lbh qb
be pnhfr gb bpphe: (n) qvfgevohgvba bs guvf be nal Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
jbex, (o) nygrengvba, zbqvsvpngvba, be nqqvgvbaf be qryrgvbaf gb nal
Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbex, naq (p) nal Qrsrpg lbh pnhfr.


Frpgvba  2.  Vasbezngvba nobhg gur Zvffvba bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz

Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz vf flabalzbhf jvgu gur serr qvfgevohgvba bs
ryrpgebavp jbexf va sbezngf ernqnoyr ol gur jvqrfg inevrgl bs pbzchgref
vapyhqvat bofbyrgr, byq, zvqqyr-ntrq naq arj pbzchgref.  Vg rkvfgf
orpnhfr bs gur rssbegf bs uhaqerqf bs ibyhagrref naq qbangvbaf sebz
crbcyr va nyy jnyxf bs yvsr.

Ibyhagrref naq svanapvny fhccbeg gb cebivqr ibyhagrref jvgu gur
nffvfgnapr gurl arrq, ner pevgvpny gb ernpuvat Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz'f
tbnyf naq rafhevat gung gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz pbyyrpgvba jvyy
erznva serryl ninvynoyr sbe trarengvbaf gb pbzr.  Va 2001, gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba jnf perngrq gb cebivqr n frpher
naq creznarag shgher sbe Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz naq shgher trarengvbaf.
Gb yrnea zber nobhg gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba
naq ubj lbhe rssbegf naq qbangvbaf pna uryc, frr Frpgvbaf 3 naq 4
naq gur Sbhaqngvba jro cntr ng uggc://jjj.ctyns.bet.


Frpgvba 3.  Vasbezngvba nobhg gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir
Sbhaqngvba
